import os
import json
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import requests

load_dotenv(override=True)

# ============================================================================
# ðŸŽ­ PERSONA TEMPORARIAMENTE DESABILITADA (Original)
# ============================================================================
PERSONA_AVAILABLE = False
print("âš ï¸ Persona temporariamente desabilitada para evitar erro de null bytes")

# ============================================================================
# ADIÃ‡ÃƒO DO PROMPT ENGINEERING
# ============================================================================
try:
    from core.prompt_engineering.prompt_engine import PromptEngineering
    PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE = True
    print("âœ… Sistema de Prompt Engineering carregado")
except ImportError as e:
    PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE = False
    print(f"âš ï¸ Prompt Engineering nÃ£o disponÃ­vel: {e}")

def load_knowledge_base():
    """Carregar base de conhecimento simples"""
    knowledge_file = "./data/knowledge_base.json"
    
    if not os.path.exists(knowledge_file):
        print("âŒ Base de conhecimento nÃ£o encontrada!")
        return []
    
    with open(knowledge_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return json.load(f)

def search_knowledge(query, knowledge_base, max_results=3):
    """Busca simples por palavras-chave"""
    query_lower = query.lower()
    results = []
    
    for item in knowledge_base:
        content_lower = item["content"].lower()
        
        # Busca simples por palavras
        score = 0
        for word in query_lower.split():
            if len(word) > 2:  # Ignorar palavras muito pequenas
                if word in content_lower:
                    score += content_lower.count(word)
        
        if score > 0:
            results.append((score, item))
    
    # Ordenar por relevÃ¢ncia
    results.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
    
    return [item for score, item in results[:max_results]]

def format_AiAmiga_response(response: str) -> str:
    """Aplicar formataÃ§Ã£o bÃ¡sica da persona AiAmiga manualmente"""
    
    # Se resposta jÃ¡ tem elementos da AiAmiga, retornar como estÃ¡
    if "aiamiga" in response.lower() or "ï¿½ï¿½" in response:
        return response
    
    # Adicionar cumprimento se nÃ£o tiver
    greeting_words = ["olÃ¡", "oi", "bom dia", "boa tarde", "boa noite"]
    has_greeting = any(word in response.lower() for word in greeting_words)
    
    if not has_greeting:
        response = "ðŸ˜Š OlÃ¡! " + response
    
    # Adicionar oferta de ajuda se nÃ£o tiver
    help_words = ["posso ajudar", "mais alguma", "outras dÃºvidas", "tem alguma outra pergunta"]
    has_help = any(word in response.lower() for word in help_words)
    
    if not has_help and len(response) > 100:
        response += "\n\nâ“ Posso ajudar com mais alguma informaÃ§Ã£o sobre o Crediamigo?"
    
    # Adicionar assinatura se nÃ£o tiver
    signature_words = ["aiamiga", "assistente virtual", "banco do nordeste"]
    has_signature = any(word in response.lower() for word in signature_words)
    
    if not has_signature:
        response += "\n\nðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"
    
    return response

# MODIFICAR A FUNÃ‡ÃƒO answer_question PARA USAR PROMPT ENGINEERING
def answer_question(question: str) -> str:
    """Responder pergunta usando base simples com Prompt Engineering avanÃ§ado"""
    try:
        print(f"ðŸ” Processando pergunta: {question[:50]}...")
        
        # Carregar base de conhecimento
        knowledge_base = load_knowledge_base()
        if not knowledge_base:
            error_msg = """ðŸ˜” Ops! A base de conhecimento nÃ£o estÃ¡ disponÃ­vel no momento.

ðŸ”§ **Para resolver:**
Execute: `python src/create_vectordb.py` primeiro.

ðŸŽ¯ **Estou aqui para ajudar com:**
- ðŸ’° Programa Crediamigo
- ðŸ“‹ DocumentaÃ§Ã£o necessÃ¡ria
- ðŸ“Š AvaliaÃ§Ã£o de carteira
- ðŸŽ“ EducaÃ§Ã£o financeira

â“ Assim que a base estiver pronta, poderei responder suas perguntas!

ðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"""
            return error_msg
        
        print(f"ðŸ“š Base carregada com {len(knowledge_base)} entradas")
        
        # Buscar contexto relevante
        relevant_docs = search_knowledge(question, knowledge_base)
        
        if not relevant_docs:
            no_info_response = """NÃ£o encontrei informaÃ§Ãµes especÃ­ficas para sua pergunta na base de conhecimento atual.

ðŸŽ¯ **Posso ajudar com informaÃ§Ãµes sobre:**
- ðŸ’° Programa Crediamigo
- ðŸ“‹ Processos e documentaÃ§Ã£o
- ðŸ“Š AvaliaÃ§Ã£o de carteira
- ðŸŽ“ EducaÃ§Ã£o financeira
- ðŸ¦ MicrocrÃ©dito

ðŸ’¡ **Dica:** Tente reformular sua pergunta ou seja mais especÃ­fico sobre o que deseja saber do Crediamigo."""
            
            return format_AiAmiga_response(no_info_response)
        
        print(f"ðŸ” Encontrados {len(relevant_docs)} documentos relevantes")
        
        # Montar contexto
        context = "\n\n".join([doc["content"] for doc in relevant_docs])
        
        # ============================================================================
        # ðŸŽ¯ USAR PROMPT ENGINEERING AVANÃ‡ADO
        # ============================================================================
        if PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE:
            # Inicializar engine de prompts
            prompt_engine = PromptEngineering()
            
            # Gerar prompt otimizado baseado no tipo de pergunta
            prompt_result = prompt_engine.get_optimized_prompt(question, context)
            
            print(f"ðŸŽ¯ Tipo de pergunta detectado: {prompt_result['question_type']}")
            print(f"ðŸ“ Prompt gerado: {len(prompt_result['prompt'])} caracteres")
            
            # Usar prompt otimizado
            optimized_prompt = prompt_result['prompt']
            temperature = prompt_result['config']['temperature']
            max_tokens = prompt_result['config']['max_tokens']
            
            # A mensagem para o LLM Ã© um Ãºnico prompt otimizado
            messages_for_llm = [
                {
                    "role": "user", 
                    "content": optimized_prompt
                }
            ]
            
        else:
            # Fallback para prompt bÃ¡sico (adaptado para AiAmiga)
            optimized_prompt_fallback = f"""VocÃª Ã© a AiAmiga, assistente do Crediamigo.
            
Contexto: {context}

Pergunta: {question}

Responda de forma clara e empÃ¡tica."""
            temperature = 0.1
            max_tokens = 500

            messages_for_llm = [
                {
                    "role": "user", 
                    "content": optimized_prompt_fallback
                }
            ]
        
        # ============================================================================
        # ðŸ¤– CHAMAR LLM COM PROMPT OTIMIZADO
        # ============================================================================
        api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
        base_url = os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL")
        model = os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "bnb-gpt-4.1-mini")
        
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        
        payload = {
            "model": model,
            "messages": messages_for_llm, # Usar as mensagens construÃ­das acima
            "max_tokens": max_tokens,    # Usar max_tokens dinÃ¢mico
            "temperature": temperature   # Usar temperature dinÃ¢mico
        }
        
        # Configurar certificados
        cert_path = r"C:\Users\F147176\certs\ca-bnb.pem"
        verify_cert = cert_path if os.path.exists(cert_path) else True
        
        response = requests.post(
            f"{base_url}/chat/completions",
            json=payload,
            headers=headers,
            timeout=60,
            verify=verify_cert
        )
        
        if response.status_code == 200:
            data = response.json()
            raw_answer = data['choices'][0]['message']['content']
            
            if PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE:
                print(f"âœ… Resposta gerada com Prompt Engineering ({prompt_result['question_type']})")
            else:
                print("âœ… Resposta gerada com prompt bÃ¡sico (Fallback AiAmiga)")
            
            # Aplicar formataÃ§Ã£o bÃ¡sica da AiAmiga
            formatted_answer = format_AiAmiga_response(raw_answer)
            
            return formatted_answer
            
        else:
            error_msg = f"Erro na API: {response.status_code}"
            print(f"âŒ {error_msg}")
            
            error_response = f"""ðŸ˜” Ops! Tive um problema tÃ©cnico ao consultar a API.

ðŸ”§ **Detalhes:** {error_msg} - Verifique a configuraÃ§Ã£o da API.

ðŸŽ¯ **Enquanto isso, posso ajudar com:**
- ðŸ’° InformaÃ§Ãµes gerais sobre o Crediamigo
- ðŸ“‹ OrientaÃ§Ãµes sobre documentaÃ§Ã£o
- ðŸ“Š Processos de avaliaÃ§Ã£o

â“ Tente novamente em alguns instantes!

ðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"""
            
            return error_response
        
    except Exception as e:
        error_msg = f"ERRO na execuÃ§Ã£o do Agente: {e}"
        print(f"âŒ {error_msg}")
        
        error_response = f"""ðŸ˜” Ops! Tive um problema tÃ©cnico interno.

ðŸ”§ **Detalhes:** {str(e)}

ðŸŽ¯ **Estou aqui para ajudar com:**
- ðŸ’° Programa Crediamigo
- ðŸ“‹ DocumentaÃ§Ã£o necessÃ¡ria
- ðŸ“Š AvaliaÃ§Ã£o de carteira
- ï¿½ï¿½ EducaÃ§Ã£o financeira

â“ Tente reformular sua pergunta ou pergunte novamente!

ðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"""
        
        return error_response

# agent_semantic_final.py - VersÃ£o final com SSL flexÃ­vel
import os
import json
import ssl
import urllib3
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import requests
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple
import numpy as np
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

load_dotenv(override=True)

# Desabilitar avisos SSL
urllib3.disable_warnings(urllib3.exceptions.InsecureRequestWarning)

def configure_ssl_flexible():
    """Configurar SSL de forma flexÃ­vel"""
    cert_path = r"C:\Users\F147176\certs\ca-bnb.pem"
    
    if os.path.exists(cert_path):
        os.environ['REQUESTS_CA_BUNDLE'] = cert_path
        os.environ['CURL_CA_BUNDLE'] = cert_path
        os.environ['SSL_CERT_FILE'] = cert_path
        print(f"âœ… Certificados configurados: {cert_path}")
        return cert_path
    else:
        print("âš ï¸ Certificado nÃ£o encontrado")
        return False

def make_api_request_flexible(url, payload, headers, timeout=60):
    """Fazer requisiÃ§Ã£o API com SSL flexÃ­vel"""
    cert_path = r"C:\Users\F147176\certs\ca-bnb.pem"
    
    # ConfiguraÃ§Ãµes SSL para tentar
    ssl_configs = [
        cert_path if os.path.exists(cert_path) else None,
        True,   # VerificaÃ§Ã£o padrÃ£o
        False   # Sem verificaÃ§Ã£o (Ãºltimo recurso)
    ]
    
    for i, verify_setting in enumerate(ssl_configs, 1):
        try:
            print(f"ðŸ”„ Tentativa SSL {i}/3...")
            
            response = requests.post(
                url,
                json=payload,
                headers=headers,
                timeout=timeout,
                verify=verify_setting
            )
            
            if response.status_code == 200:
                print(f"âœ… Sucesso com SSL config {i}")
                return response
            else:
                print(f"âŒ Status {response.status_code}")
                
        except requests.exceptions.SSLError:
            print(f"âŒ Erro SSL na tentativa {i}")
            continue
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro na tentativa {i}: {str(e)[:50]}...")
            continue
    
    raise Exception("Todas as configuraÃ§Ãµes SSL falharam")

# Configurar SSL
configure_ssl_flexible()

print("âš ï¸ Persona temporariamente desabilitada para evitar erro de null bytes")
print("âœ… Busca SemÃ¢ntica Local disponÃ­vel (TF-IDF)")

# ============================================================================
# ðŸ” CLASSE DE BUSCA SEMÃ‚NTICA LOCAL (TESTADA E FUNCIONANDO)
# ============================================================================
class LocalSemanticSearchEngine:
    """Motor de busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.vectorizer = None
        self.document_vectors = None
        self.documents = []
        self.initialized = False
        
    def initialize(self, knowledge_base: List[Dict]) -> bool:
        """Inicializar sistema de busca semÃ¢ntica local"""
        if self.initialized:
            return True
        
        try:
            self.documents = knowledge_base
            
            print(f"ðŸ”„ Criando Ã­ndice TF-IDF para {len(knowledge_base)} documentos...")
            
            texts = [doc.get("content", "") for doc in knowledge_base]
            
            self.vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer(
                max_features=5000,
                ngram_range=(1, 2),
                lowercase=True,
                min_df=1,
                max_df=0.95
            )
            
            self.document_vectors = self.vectorizer.fit_transform(texts)
            
            self.initialized = True
            print(f"âœ… Sistema TF-IDF inicializado! Vetores: {self.document_vectors.shape}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro ao inicializar TF-IDF: {e}")
            return False
    
    def search(self, query: str, top_k: int = 5, min_similarity: float = 0.05) -> List[Tuple[float, Dict]]:
        """Busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
        if not self.initialized:
            return []
        
        try:
            query_vector = self.vectorizer.transform([query])
            similarities = cosine_similarity(query_vector, self.document_vectors).flatten()
            top_indices = similarities.argsort()[-top_k:][::-1]
            
            results = []
            for idx in top_indices:
                similarity = similarities[idx]
                if similarity >= min_similarity:
                    results.append((float(similarity), self.documents[idx]))
            
            return results
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro na busca TF-IDF: {e}")
            return []

# InstÃ¢ncia global
_semantic_engine = None

def get_semantic_engine() -> Optional[LocalSemanticSearchEngine]:
    """Obter instÃ¢ncia do motor semÃ¢ntico"""
    global _semantic_engine
    if _semantic_engine is None:
        _semantic_engine = LocalSemanticSearchEngine()
    return _semantic_engine

def load_knowledge_base():
    """Carregar base de conhecimento"""
    knowledge_file = "./data/knowledge_base.json"
    
    if not os.path.exists(knowledge_file):
        print("âŒ Base de conhecimento nÃ£o encontrada!")
        return []
    
    with open(knowledge_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return json.load(f)

def search_knowledge_semantic(query, knowledge_base, max_results=5):
    """Busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
    semantic_engine = get_semantic_engine()
    
    if not semantic_engine.initialized:
        print("ðŸ”„ Inicializando busca semÃ¢ntica...")
        if not semantic_engine.initialize(knowledge_base):
            return []
    
    semantic_results = semantic_engine.search(query, top_k=max_results, min_similarity=0.05)
    
    if semantic_results:
        print(f"ðŸ§  Busca TF-IDF: {len(semantic_results)} resultados")
        for i, (score, doc) in enumerate(semantic_results, 1):
            source = doc.get('source', 'N/A')
            print(f"  ðŸ“„ {i}. Score: {score:.3f} - {source[:50]}...")
        
        return [doc for score, doc in semantic_results]
    else:
        return []

def format_AiAmiga_response(response: str) -> str:
    """Aplicar formataÃ§Ã£o da AiAmiga"""
    if "aiamiga" in response.lower() or "ðŸ¤–" in response:
        return response
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["olÃ¡", "oi", "bom dia"]):
        response = "ðŸ˜Š OlÃ¡! " + response
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["posso ajudar", "mais alguma"]):
        response += "\n\nâ“ Posso ajudar com mais alguma informaÃ§Ã£o sobre o Crediamigo?"
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["aiamiga", "assistente virtual"]):
        response += "\n\nðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"
    
    return response

def answer_question(question: str) -> str:
    """Responder pergunta usando busca semÃ¢ntica + API"""
    try:
        print(f"ðŸ” Processando pergunta: {question[:50]}...")
        
        knowledge_base = load_knowledge_base()
        if not knowledge_base:
            return format_AiAmiga_response("Base de conhecimento nÃ£o disponÃ­vel.")
        
        print(f"ðŸ“š Base carregada com {len(knowledge_base)} entradas")
        
        # Buscar usando TF-IDF
        relevant_docs = search_knowledge_semantic(question, knowledge_base, max_results=5)
        
        if not relevant_docs:
            return format_AiAmiga_response("NÃ£o encontrei informaÃ§Ãµes especÃ­ficas para sua pergunta.")
        
        print(f"ðŸ” Encontrados {len(relevant_docs)} documentos relevantes")
        
        # Montar contexto
        context = "\n\n".join([doc["content"] for doc in relevant_docs])
        
        # Prompt otimizado
        prompt = f"""VocÃª Ã© a AiAmiga, assistente especializada do Programa Crediamigo do Banco do Nordeste.

Contexto relevante encontrado pela busca semÃ¢ntica:
{context}

Pergunta do usuÃ¡rio: {question}

Responda de forma clara, empÃ¡tica e profissional, baseando-se apenas no contexto fornecido."""
        
        # Chamar API com SSL flexÃ­vel
        api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
        base_url = os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL")
        model = os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "bnb-gpt-4.1-mini")
        
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        
        payload = {
            "model": model,
            "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
            "max_tokens": 500,
            "temperature": 0.1
        }
        
        # Usar funÃ§Ã£o SSL flexÃ­vel
        response = make_api_request_flexible(
            f"{base_url}/chat/completions",
            payload,
            headers
        )
        
        if response.status_code == 200:
            data = response.json()
            raw_answer = data['choices'][0]['message']['content']
            
            # Adicionar info sobre busca semÃ¢ntica
            search_info = "\n\nðŸ§  *Resposta gerada com busca semÃ¢ntica TF-IDF*"
            
            print("âœ… Resposta gerada com sucesso!")
            
            return format_AiAmiga_response(raw_answer + search_info)
        else:
            return format_AiAmiga_response(f"Erro na API: {response.status_code}")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ Erro: {e}")
        return format_AiAmiga_response(f"Problema tÃ©cnico: {str(e)}")

# agent_semantic_hybrid.txt
# src/core/agent_semantic_hybrid.py
import os
import json
import time
import certifi
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import requests
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple

load_dotenv(override=True)

PERSONA_AVAILABLE = False
print("âš ï¸ Persona temporariamente desabilitada para evitar erro de null bytes")

# Busca SemÃ¢ntica Local (TF-IDF)
SEMANTIC_SEARCH_AVAILABLE = False
try:
    import numpy as np
    from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
    from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
    SEMANTIC_SEARCH_AVAILABLE = True
    print("âœ… Busca SemÃ¢ntica Local disponÃ­vel (TF-IDF)")
except ImportError as e:
    print(f"âš ï¸ Busca SemÃ¢ntica nÃ£o disponÃ­vel: {e}")
    print("ðŸ’¡ Para ativar: pip install scikit-learn numpy")

# Prompt Engineering (opcional)
try:
    import sys
    sys.path.append('.')
    from core.prompt_engineering.prompt_engine import PromptEngineering
    PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE = True
    print("âœ… Sistema de Prompt Engineering carregado")
except ImportError as e:
    PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE = False
    print(f"âš ï¸ Prompt Engineering nÃ£o disponÃ­vel: {e}")

class LocalSemanticSearchEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.vectorizer = None
        self.document_vectors = None
        self.documents = []
        self.initialized = False

    def initialize(self, knowledge_base: List[Dict]) -> bool:
        if self.initialized:
            return True
        try:
            self.documents = knowledge_base
            print(f"ðŸ”„ Criando Ã­ndice TF-IDF para {len(knowledge_base)} documentos...")
            texts = [doc.get("content", "") for doc in knowledge_base]
            self.vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer(
                max_features=5000,
                stop_words=None,
                ngram_range=(1, 2),
                lowercase=True,
                min_df=1,
                max_df=0.95
            )
            self.document_vectors = self.vectorizer.fit_transform(texts)
            self.initialized = True
            print("âœ… Sistema de busca TF-IDF inicializado!")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro ao inicializar busca TF-IDF: {e}")
            return False

    def search(self, query: str, top_k: int = 5, min_similarity: float = 0.05) -> List[Tuple[float, Dict]]:
        if not self.initialized:
            return []
        try:
            query_vector = self.vectorizer.transform([query])
            similarities = cosine_similarity(query_vector, self.document_vectors).flatten()
            top_indices = similarities.argsort()[-top_k:][::-1]
            results = []
            for idx in top_indices:
                similarity = float(similarities[idx])
                if similarity >= min_similarity:
                    results.append((similarity, self.documents[idx]))
            return results
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro na busca TF-IDF: {e}")
            return []

_local_semantic_engine = None
def get_local_semantic_engine() -> Optional[LocalSemanticSearchEngine]:
    global _local_semantic_engine
    if _local_semantic_engine is None and SEMANTIC_SEARCH_AVAILABLE:
        _local_semantic_engine = LocalSemanticSearchEngine()
    return _local_semantic_engine

def load_knowledge_base() -> List[Dict]:
    knowledge_file = "./data/knowledge_base.json"
    if not os.path.exists(knowledge_file):
        print("âŒ Base de conhecimento nÃ£o encontrada!")
        return []
    with open(knowledge_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return json.load(f)

def search_knowledge_keyword(query: str, knowledge_base: List[Dict], max_results: int = 3) -> List[Dict]:
    query_lower = query.lower()
    results = []
    for item in knowledge_base:
        content_lower = item.get("content", "").lower()
        score = 0
        for word in query_lower.split():
            if len(word) > 2 and word in content_lower:
                score += content_lower.count(word)
        if score > 0:
            results.append((score, item))
    results.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
    return [item for score, item in results[:max_results]]

def search_knowledge_semantic_local(query: str, knowledge_base: List[Dict], max_results: int = 5) -> List[Dict]:
    semantic_engine = get_local_semantic_engine()
    if not semantic_engine:
        print("âš ï¸ Busca semÃ¢ntica local nÃ£o disponÃ­vel, usando busca por palavras-chave")
        return search_knowledge_keyword(query, knowledge_base, max_results)
    if not semantic_engine.initialized:
        print("ðŸ”„ Inicializando busca semÃ¢ntica local...")
        if not semantic_engine.initialize(knowledge_base):
            print("âŒ Falha na inicializaÃ§Ã£o, usando busca por palavras-chave")
            return search_knowledge_keyword(query, knowledge_base, max_results)
    semantic_results = semantic_engine.search(query, top_k=max_results, min_similarity=0.05)
    if semantic_results:
        print(f"ðŸ§  Busca TF-IDF: {len(semantic_results)} resultados")
        for i, (score, doc) in enumerate(semantic_results, 1):
            source = doc.get('source', 'N/A')
            print(f"  ðŸ“„ {i}. Score: {score:.3f} - {source[:60]}...")
        return [doc for score, doc in semantic_results]
    print("âš ï¸ Busca TF-IDF sem resultados, usando busca por palavras-chave")
    return search_knowledge_keyword(query, knowledge_base, max_results)

def search_knowledge_hybrid(query: str, knowledge_base: List[Dict], max_results: int = 5, use_semantic: bool = True) -> List[Dict]:
    if use_semantic and SEMANTIC_SEARCH_AVAILABLE:
        semantic_results = search_knowledge_semantic_local(query, knowledge_base, max_results)
        if semantic_results:
            return semantic_results
    print("ðŸ”¤ Usando busca por palavras-chave")
    return search_knowledge_keyword(query, knowledge_base, max_results)

def format_AiAmiga_response(response: str) -> str:
    if "aiamiga" in response.lower() or "ðŸ¤–" in response:
        return response
    greeting_words = ["olÃ¡", "oi", "bom dia", "boa tarde", "boa noite"]
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in greeting_words):
        response = "ðŸ˜Š OlÃ¡! " + response
    help_words = ["posso ajudar", "mais alguma", "outras dÃºvidas", "tem alguma outra pergunta"]
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in help_words) and len(response) > 100:
        response += "\n\nâ“ Posso ajudar com mais alguma informaÃ§Ã£o sobre o Crediamigo?"
    signature_words = ["aiamiga", "assistente virtual", "banco do nordeste"]
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in signature_words):
        response += "\n\nðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"
    return response

def answer_question(question: str, use_semantic: bool = True) -> str:
    try:
        print(f"ðŸ” Processando pergunta: {question[:50]}...")
        knowledge_base = load_knowledge_base()
        if not knowledge_base:
            return """ðŸ˜” Ops! A base de conhecimento nÃ£o estÃ¡ disponÃ­vel no momento.

ðŸ”§ Para resolver:
Execute: `python src/create_vectordb.py` primeiro.

ðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"""

        print(f"ðŸ“š Base carregada com {len(knowledge_base)} entradas")
        relevant_docs = search_knowledge_hybrid(question, knowledge_base, max_results=5, use_semantic=use_semantic)
        if not relevant_docs:
            no_info_response = """NÃ£o encontrei informaÃ§Ãµes especÃ­ficas para sua pergunta na base de conhecimento atual.

ðŸŽ¯ Posso ajudar com:
- ðŸ’° Programa Crediamigo
- ðŸ“‹ Processos e documentaÃ§Ã£o
- ðŸ“Š AvaliaÃ§Ã£o de carteira
- ðŸŽ“ EducaÃ§Ã£o financeira
- ðŸ¦ MicrocrÃ©dito"""
            return format_AiAmiga_response(no_info_response)

        print(f"ðŸ” Encontrados {len(relevant_docs)} documentos relevantes")
        context = "\n\n".join([doc.get("content", "") for doc in relevant_docs])

        if PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE:
            prompt_engine = PromptEngineering()
            prompt_result = prompt_engine.get_optimized_prompt(question, context)
            optimized_prompt = prompt_result['prompt']
            temperature = prompt_result['config']['temperature']
            max_tokens = prompt_result['config']['max_tokens']
            messages_for_llm = [{"role": "user", "content": optimized_prompt}]
        else:
            optimized_prompt = f"""VocÃª Ã© a AiAmiga, assistente especializada do Programa Crediamigo do Banco do Nordeste.

Contexto relevante:
{context}

Pergunta do usuÃ¡rio: {question}

Responda de forma clara, empÃ¡tica e profissional, baseando-se apenas no contexto fornecido."""
            temperature = 0.1
            max_tokens = 500
            messages_for_llm = [{"role": "user", "content": optimized_prompt}]

        api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
        base_url = os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL")
        model = os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "bnb-gpt-4.1-mini")
        if not api_key or not base_url:
            return "ConfiguraÃ§Ã£o de API ausente. Defina OPENAI_API_KEY e OPENAI_BASE_URL."

        headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}", "Content-Type": "application/json"}
        payload = {"model": model, "messages": messages_for_llm, "max_tokens": max_tokens, "temperature": temperature}

        # ForÃ§ar uso do bundle pÃºblico (certifi) atÃ© corrigir a CA corporativa
        verify_path = certifi.where()
        print(f"ðŸ” Usando bundle padrÃ£o (certifi): {verify_path}")

        try:
            response = requests.post(
                f"{base_url}/chat/completions",
                json=payload,
                headers=headers,
                timeout=60,
                verify=verify_path
            )
        except requests.exceptions.SSLError as ssl_err:
            print(f"âŒ SSLError: {ssl_err}")
            return f"""ðŸ˜” Problema de verificaÃ§Ã£o TLS com o endpoint.

ðŸ”§ Dicas:
- Tente novamente usando o bundle padrÃ£o (certifi) â€” jÃ¡ habilitado.
- Se sua rede exigir CA corporativa, atualize o arquivo com intermediÃ¡rios + raiz corretos.

Detalhes: {ssl_err}

ðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"""

        if response.status_code == 200:
            data = response.json()
            raw_answer = data['choices'][0]['message']['content']
            search_info = "\n\nðŸ§  *Resposta gerada com busca semÃ¢ntica TF-IDF*" if (use_semantic and SEMANTIC_SEARCH_AVAILABLE) else "\n\nðŸ”¤ *Resposta gerada com busca por palavras-chave*"
            print("âœ… Resposta gerada com sucesso")
            return format_AiAmiga_response(raw_answer + search_info)

        print(f"âŒ Erro na API: {response.status_code} - {response.text[:200]}")
        return f"""ðŸ˜” Ops! Tive um problema tÃ©cnico ao consultar a API.

ðŸ”§ CÃ³digo HTTP: {response.status_code}
ðŸ” Endpoint: {base_url}/chat/completions

Verifique:
- Chave e URL (OPENAI_API_KEY, OPENAI_BASE_URL)
- Rede/VPN

ðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"""

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ ERRO na execuÃ§Ã£o do Agente: {e}")
        return f"""ðŸ˜” Ops! Tive um problema tÃ©cnico interno.

ðŸ”§ Detalhes: {str(e)}

ðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"""

def get_search_stats() -> Dict[str, Any]:
    stats = {
        "semantic_available": SEMANTIC_SEARCH_AVAILABLE,
        "prompt_engineering_available": PROMPT_ENGINEERING_AVAILABLE,
        "knowledge_base_loaded": len(load_knowledge_base()) > 0
    }
    if SEMANTIC_SEARCH_AVAILABLE:
        semantic_engine = get_local_semantic_engine()
        if semantic_engine:
            stats["semantic_initialized"] = semantic_engine.initialized
            stats["semantic_documents"] = len(semantic_engine.documents)
    return stats

if __name__ == "__main__":

import os
import json
import ssl
import urllib3
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import requests
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple
import numpy as np
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

load_dotenv(override=True)

# Desabilitar avisos SSL
urllib3.disable_warnings(urllib3.exceptions.InsecureRequestWarning)

def configure_ssl_flexible():
    """Configurar SSL de forma flexÃ­vel"""
    cert_path = r"C:\Users\F147176\certs\ca-bnb.pem"
    
    if os.path.exists(cert_path):
        os.environ['REQUESTS_CA_BUNDLE'] = cert_path
        os.environ['CURL_CA_BUNDLE'] = cert_path
        os.environ['SSL_CERT_FILE'] = cert_path
        print(f"âœ… Certificados configurados: {cert_path}")
        return cert_path
    else:
        print("âš ï¸ Certificado nÃ£o encontrado")
        return False

def make_api_request_flexible(url, payload, headers, timeout=60):
    """Fazer requisiÃ§Ã£o API com SSL flexÃ­vel"""
    cert_path = r"C:\Users\F147176\certs\ca-bnb.pem"
    
    # ConfiguraÃ§Ãµes SSL para tentar
    ssl_configs = [
        cert_path if os.path.exists(cert_path) else None,
        True,   # VerificaÃ§Ã£o padrÃ£o
        False   # Sem verificaÃ§Ã£o (Ãºltimo recurso)
    ]
    
    for i, verify_setting in enumerate(ssl_configs, 1):
        try:
            print(f"ðŸ”„ Tentativa SSL {i}/3...")
            
            response = requests.post(
                url,
                json=payload,
                headers=headers,
                timeout=timeout,
                verify=verify_setting
            )
            
            if response.status_code == 200:
                print(f"âœ… Sucesso com SSL config {i}")
                return response
            else:
                print(f"âŒ Status {response.status_code}")
                
        except requests.exceptions.SSLError:
            print(f"âŒ Erro SSL na tentativa {i}")
            continue
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro na tentativa {i}: {str(e)[:50]}...")
            continue
    
    raise Exception("Todas as configuraÃ§Ãµes SSL falharam")

# Configurar SSL
configure_ssl_flexible()

print("âš ï¸ Persona temporariamente desabilitada para evitar erro de null bytes")
print("âœ… Busca SemÃ¢ntica Local disponÃ­vel (TF-IDF)")

# ============================================================================
# ðŸ” CLASSE DE BUSCA SEMÃ‚NTICA LOCAL (TESTADA E FUNCIONANDO)
# ============================================================================
class LocalSemanticSearchEngine:
    """Motor de busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.vectorizer = None
        self.document_vectors = None
        self.documents = []
        self.initialized = False
        
    def initialize(self, knowledge_base: List[Dict]) -> bool:
        """Inicializar sistema de busca semÃ¢ntica local"""
        if self.initialized:
            return True
        
        try:
            self.documents = knowledge_base
            
            print(f"ðŸ”„ Criando Ã­ndice TF-IDF para {len(knowledge_base)} documentos...")
            
            texts = [doc.get("content", "") for doc in knowledge_base]
            
            self.vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer(
                max_features=5000,
                ngram_range=(1, 2),
                lowercase=True,
                min_df=1,
                max_df=0.95
            )
            
            self.document_vectors = self.vectorizer.fit_transform(texts)
            
            self.initialized = True
            print(f"âœ… Sistema TF-IDF inicializado! Vetores: {self.document_vectors.shape}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro ao inicializar TF-IDF: {e}")
            return False
    
    def search(self, query: str, top_k: int = 5, min_similarity: float = 0.05) -> List[Tuple[float, Dict]]:
        """Busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
        if not self.initialized:
            return []
        
        try:
            query_vector = self.vectorizer.transform([query])
            similarities = cosine_similarity(query_vector, self.document_vectors).flatten()
            top_indices = similarities.argsort()[-top_k:][::-1]
            
            results = []
            for idx in top_indices:
                similarity = similarities[idx]
                if similarity >= min_similarity:
                    results.append((float(similarity), self.documents[idx]))
            
            return results
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro na busca TF-IDF: {e}")
            return []

# InstÃ¢ncia global
_semantic_engine = None

def get_semantic_engine() -> Optional[LocalSemanticSearchEngine]:
    """Obter instÃ¢ncia do motor semÃ¢ntico"""
    global _semantic_engine
    if _semantic_engine is None:
        _semantic_engine = LocalSemanticSearchEngine()
    return _semantic_engine

def load_knowledge_base():
    """Carregar base de conhecimento"""
    knowledge_file = "./data/knowledge_base.json"
    
    if not os.path.exists(knowledge_file):
        print("âŒ Base de conhecimento nÃ£o encontrada!")
        return []
    
    with open(knowledge_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return json.load(f)

def search_knowledge_semantic(query, knowledge_base, max_results=5):
    """Busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
    semantic_engine = get_semantic_engine()
    
    if not semantic_engine.initialized:
        print("ðŸ”„ Inicializando busca semÃ¢ntica...")
        if not semantic_engine.initialize(knowledge_base):
            return []
    
    semantic_results = semantic_engine.search(query, top_k=max_results, min_similarity=0.05)
    
    if semantic_results:
        print(f"ðŸ§  Busca TF-IDF: {len(semantic_results)} resultados")
        for i, (score, doc) in enumerate(semantic_results, 1):
            source = doc.get('source', 'N/A')
            print(f"  ðŸ“„ {i}. Score: {score:.3f} - {source[:50]}...")
        
        return [doc for score, doc in semantic_results]
    else:
        return []

def format_AiAmiga_response(response: str) -> str:
    """Aplicar formataÃ§Ã£o da AiAmiga"""
    if "aiamiga" in response.lower() or "ðŸ¤–" in response:
        return response
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["olÃ¡", "oi", "bom dia"]):
        response = "ðŸ˜Š OlÃ¡! " + response
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["posso ajudar", "mais alguma"]):
        response += "\n\nâ“ Posso ajudar com mais alguma informaÃ§Ã£o sobre o Crediamigo?"
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["aiamiga", "assistente virtual"]):
        response += "\n\nðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"
    
    return response

def answer_question(question: str) -> str:
    """Responder pergunta usando busca semÃ¢ntica + API"""
    try:
        print(f"ðŸ” Processando pergunta: {question[:50]}...")
        
        knowledge_base = load_knowledge_base()
        if not knowledge_base:
            return format_AiAmiga_response("Base de conhecimento nÃ£o disponÃ­vel.")
        
        print(f"ðŸ“š Base carregada com {len(knowledge_base)} entradas")
        
        # Buscar usando TF-IDF
        relevant_docs = search_knowledge_semantic(question, knowledge_base, max_results=5)
        
        if not relevant_docs:
            return format_AiAmiga_response("NÃ£o encontrei informaÃ§Ãµes especÃ­ficas para sua pergunta.")
        
        print(f"ðŸ” Encontrados {len(relevant_docs)} documentos relevantes")
        
        # Montar contexto
        context = "\n\n".join([doc["content"] for doc in relevant_docs])
        
        # Prompt otimizado
        prompt = f"""VocÃª Ã© a AiAmiga, assistente especializada do Programa Crediamigo do Banco do Nordeste.

Contexto relevante encontrado pela busca semÃ¢ntica:
{context}

Pergunta do usuÃ¡rio: {question}

Responda de forma clara, empÃ¡tica e profissional, baseando-se apenas no contexto fornecido."""
        
        # Chamar API com SSL flexÃ­vel
        api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
        base_url = os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL")
        model = os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "bnb-gpt-4.1-mini")
        
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        
        payload = {
            "model": model,
            "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
            "max_tokens": 500,
            "temperature": 0.1
        }
        
        # Usar funÃ§Ã£o SSL flexÃ­vel
        response = make_api_request_flexible(
            f"{base_url}/chat/completions",
            payload,
            headers
        )
        
        if response.status_code == 200:
            data = response.json()
            raw_answer = data['choices'][0]['message']['content']
            
            # Adicionar info sobre busca semÃ¢ntica
            search_info = "\n\nðŸ§  *Resposta gerada com busca semÃ¢ntica TF-IDF*"
            
            print("âœ… Resposta gerada com sucesso!")
            
            return format_AiAmiga_response(raw_answer + search_info)
        else:
            return format_AiAmiga_response(f"Erro na API: {response.status_code}")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ Erro: {e}")
        return format_AiAmiga_response(f"Problema tÃ©cnico: {str(e)}")

    print("ðŸ§ª Testando Agent Final com Busca SemÃ¢ntica + API...")
    print("=" * 70)

    print(f"Resposta:\n{response}")
    
    print("\nâœ… Agent final funcionando!")

# agent_semantic_final.py - VersÃ£o final com SSL flexÃ­vel
import os
import json
import ssl
import urllib3
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import requests
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple
import numpy as np
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

load_dotenv(override=True)

# Desabilitar avisos SSL
urllib3.disable_warnings(urllib3.exceptions.InsecureRequestWarning)

def configure_ssl_flexible():
    """Configurar SSL de forma flexÃ­vel"""
    cert_path = r"C:\Users\F147176\certs\ca-bnb.pem"
    
    if os.path.exists(cert_path):
        os.environ['REQUESTS_CA_BUNDLE'] = cert_path
        os.environ['CURL_CA_BUNDLE'] = cert_path
        os.environ['SSL_CERT_FILE'] = cert_path
        print(f"âœ… Certificados configurados: {cert_path}")
        return cert_path
    else:
        print("âš ï¸ Certificado nÃ£o encontrado")
        return False

def make_api_request_flexible(url, payload, headers, timeout=60):
    """Fazer requisiÃ§Ã£o API com SSL flexÃ­vel"""
    cert_path = r"C:\Users\F147176\certs\ca-bnb.pem"
    
    # ConfiguraÃ§Ãµes SSL para tentar
    ssl_configs = [
        cert_path if os.path.exists(cert_path) else None,
        True,   # VerificaÃ§Ã£o padrÃ£o
        False   # Sem verificaÃ§Ã£o (Ãºltimo recurso)
    ]
    
    for i, verify_setting in enumerate(ssl_configs, 1):
        try:
            print(f"ðŸ”„ Tentativa SSL {i}/3...")
            
            response = requests.post(
                url,
                json=payload,
                headers=headers,
                timeout=timeout,
                verify=verify_setting
            )
            
            if response.status_code == 200:
                print(f"âœ… Sucesso com SSL config {i}")
                return response
            else:
                print(f"âŒ Status {response.status_code}")
                
        except requests.exceptions.SSLError:
            print(f"âŒ Erro SSL na tentativa {i}")
            continue
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro na tentativa {i}: {str(e)[:50]}...")
            continue
    
    raise Exception("Todas as configuraÃ§Ãµes SSL falharam")

# Configurar SSL
configure_ssl_flexible()

print("âš ï¸ Persona temporariamente desabilitada para evitar erro de null bytes")
print("âœ… Busca SemÃ¢ntica Local disponÃ­vel (TF-IDF)")

# ============================================================================
# ðŸ” CLASSE DE BUSCA SEMÃ‚NTICA LOCAL (TESTADA E FUNCIONANDO)
# ============================================================================
class LocalSemanticSearchEngine:
    """Motor de busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.vectorizer = None
        self.document_vectors = None
        self.documents = []
        self.initialized = False
        
    def initialize(self, knowledge_base: List[Dict]) -> bool:
        """Inicializar sistema de busca semÃ¢ntica local"""
        if self.initialized:
            return True
        
        try:
            self.documents = knowledge_base
            
            print(f"ðŸ”„ Criando Ã­ndice TF-IDF para {len(knowledge_base)} documentos...")
            
            texts = [doc.get("content", "") for doc in knowledge_base]
            
            self.vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer(
                max_features=5000,
                ngram_range=(1, 2),
                lowercase=True,
                min_df=1,
                max_df=0.95
            )
            
            self.document_vectors = self.vectorizer.fit_transform(texts)
            
            self.initialized = True
            print(f"âœ… Sistema TF-IDF inicializado! Vetores: {self.document_vectors.shape}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro ao inicializar TF-IDF: {e}")
            return False
    
    def search(self, query: str, top_k: int = 5, min_similarity: float = 0.05) -> List[Tuple[float, Dict]]:
        """Busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
        if not self.initialized:
            return []
        
        try:
            query_vector = self.vectorizer.transform([query])
            similarities = cosine_similarity(query_vector, self.document_vectors).flatten()
            top_indices = similarities.argsort()[-top_k:][::-1]
            
            results = []
            for idx in top_indices:
                similarity = similarities[idx]
                if similarity >= min_similarity:
                    results.append((float(similarity), self.documents[idx]))
            
            return results
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"âŒ Erro na busca TF-IDF: {e}")
            return []

# InstÃ¢ncia global
_semantic_engine = None

def get_semantic_engine() -> Optional[LocalSemanticSearchEngine]:
    """Obter instÃ¢ncia do motor semÃ¢ntico"""
    global _semantic_engine
    if _semantic_engine is None:
        _semantic_engine = LocalSemanticSearchEngine()
    return _semantic_engine

def load_knowledge_base():
    """Carregar base de conhecimento"""
    knowledge_file = "./data/knowledge_base.json"
    
    if not os.path.exists(knowledge_file):
        print("âŒ Base de conhecimento nÃ£o encontrada!")
        return []
    
    with open(knowledge_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return json.load(f)

def search_knowledge_semantic(query, knowledge_base, max_results=5):
    """Busca semÃ¢ntica usando TF-IDF"""
    semantic_engine = get_semantic_engine()
    
    if not semantic_engine.initialized:
        print("ðŸ”„ Inicializando busca semÃ¢ntica...")
        if not semantic_engine.initialize(knowledge_base):
            return []
    
    semantic_results = semantic_engine.search(query, top_k=max_results, min_similarity=0.05)
    
    if semantic_results:
        print(f"ðŸ§  Busca TF-IDF: {len(semantic_results)} resultados")
        for i, (score, doc) in enumerate(semantic_results, 1):
            source = doc.get('source', 'N/A')
            print(f"  ðŸ“„ {i}. Score: {score:.3f} - {source[:50]}...")
        
        return [doc for score, doc in semantic_results]
    else:
        return []

def format_AiAmiga_response(response: str) -> str:
    """Aplicar formataÃ§Ã£o da AiAmiga"""
    if "aiamiga" in response.lower() or "ðŸ¤–" in response:
        return response
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["olÃ¡", "oi", "bom dia"]):
        response = "ðŸ˜Š OlÃ¡! " + response
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["posso ajudar", "mais alguma"]):
        response += "\n\nâ“ Posso ajudar com mais alguma informaÃ§Ã£o sobre o Crediamigo?"
    
    if not any(word in response.lower() for word in ["aiamiga", "assistente virtual"]):
        response += "\n\nðŸ¤– **AiAmiga** - Assistente Virtual do Crediamigo"
    
    return response

def answer_question(question: str) -> str:
    """Responder pergunta usando busca semÃ¢ntica + API"""
    try:
        print(f"ðŸ” Processando pergunta: {question[:50]}...")
        
        knowledge_base = load_knowledge_base()
        if not knowledge_base:
            return format_AiAmiga_response("Base de conhecimento nÃ£o disponÃ­vel.")
        
        print(f"ðŸ“š Base carregada com {len(knowledge_base)} entradas")
        
        # Buscar usando TF-IDF
        relevant_docs = search_knowledge_semantic(question, knowledge_base, max_results=5)
        
        if not relevant_docs:
            return format_AiAmiga_response("NÃ£o encontrei informaÃ§Ãµes especÃ­ficas para sua pergunta.")
        
        print(f"ðŸ” Encontrados {len(relevant_docs)} documentos relevantes")
        
        # Montar contexto
        context = "\n\n".join([doc["content"] for doc in relevant_docs])
        
        # Prompt otimizado
        prompt = f"""VocÃª Ã© a AiAmiga, assistente especializada do Programa Crediamigo do Banco do Nordeste.

Contexto relevante encontrado pela busca semÃ¢ntica:
{context}

Pergunta do usuÃ¡rio: {question}

Responda de forma clara, empÃ¡tica e profissional, baseando-se apenas no contexto fornecido."""
        
        # Chamar API com SSL flexÃ­vel
        api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
        base_url = os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL")
        model = os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "bnb-gpt-4.1-mini")
        
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        
        payload = {
            "model": model,
            "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
            "max_tokens": 500,
            "temperature": 0.1
        }
        
        # Usar funÃ§Ã£o SSL flexÃ­vel
        response = make_api_request_flexible(
            f"{base_url}/chat/completions",
            payload,
            headers
        )
        
        if response.status_code == 200:
            data = response.json()
            raw_answer = data['choices'][0]['message']['content']
            
            # Adicionar info sobre busca semÃ¢ntica
            search_info = "\n\nðŸ§  *Resposta gerada com busca semÃ¢ntica TF-IDF*"
            
            print("âœ… Resposta gerada com sucesso!")
            
            return format_AiAmiga_response(raw_answer + search_info)
        else:
            return format_AiAmiga_response(f"Erro na API: {response.status_code}")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ Erro: {e}")
        return format_AiAmiga_response(f"Problema tÃ©cnico: {str(e)}")

    print("ðŸ§ª Testando Agent Final com Busca SemÃ¢ntica + API...")
    print("=" * 70)

    print(f"Resposta:\n{response}")
    
    print("\nâœ… Agent final funcionando!")

# src/core/config.py
from pathlib import Path
import os

class Config:
    BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
    ENV_PATH = BASE_DIR / ".env"

    DATA_PATH = BASE_DIR / "data" / "docs"
    CHROMA_PATH = BASE_DIR / "chroma"

    CHUNK_SIZE = int(os.getenv("CHUNK_SIZE", "1500"))
    CHUNK_OVERLAP = int(os.getenv("CHUNK_OVERLAP", "200"))
    SUPPORTED_EXTENSIONS = {".pdf", ".txt", ".docx", ".pptx", ".html", ".md"}

    # Modelos
    # Prioriza OPENAI_MODEL; se nÃ£o houver, usa LLM_MODEL; senÃ£o fallback padrÃ£o.
    LLM_MODEL = (
        os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL")
        or os.getenv("LLM_MODEL")
        or "gpt-4o-mini"
    )
    TEMPERATURE = float(os.getenv("LLM_TEMPERATURE", "0.1"))

    # OpenAI / Proxy
    OPENAI_ENV_VAR = os.getenv("OPENAI_ENV_VAR", "OPENAI_API_KEY")
    OPENAI_BASE_URL = os.getenv("OPENAI_BASE_URL", "").strip()

    @staticmethod
    def ensure_dirs() -> None:
        Config.DATA_PATH.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Config.CHROMA_PATH.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)


# embedding.txt
# src/AiAmiga/core/embedding.py (VersÃ£o Refatorada)
import hashlib
import time
from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Optional, Set
import json

from langchain_openai import OpenAIEmbeddings
from langchain_core.documents import Document

try:
    from langchain_chroma import Chroma
except ImportError:
    from langchain_community.vectorstores import Chroma

from AiAmiga.core.config import settings
from AiAmiga.core.loader import DocumentLoader
from AiAmiga.utils.exceptions import EmbeddingError, VectorStoreError
from AiAmiga.utils.logger import setup_logger

logger = setup_logger(__name__)

class EmbeddingManager:
    """Gerenciador de embeddings e vector store."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.embeddings: Optional[OpenAIEmbeddings] = None
        self.vector_store: Optional[Chroma] = None
        self.metrics = EmbeddingMetrics()
        
    def _validate_environment(self) -> None:
        """Valida configuraÃ§Ãµes necessÃ¡rias."""
        if not settings.openai_api_key:
            raise EmbeddingError("OPENAI_API_KEY nÃ£o configurado")
            
        if settings.openai_base_url:
            logger.info(f"Usando base URL customizada: {settings.openai_base_url}")
        
        # Criar diretÃ³rio do Chroma se nÃ£o existir
        settings.chroma_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    
    def initialize_embeddings(self) -> OpenAIEmbeddings:
        """Inicializa cliente de embeddings."""
        self._validate_environment()
        
        try:
            self.embeddings = OpenAIEmbeddings(
                model=settings.embedding_model,
                openai_api_base=settings.openai_base_url,
                openai_api_key=settings.openai_api_key,
            )
            
            # Teste de conectividade
            _ = self.embeddings.embed_query("teste de conectividade")
            logger.info("âœ… Embedding API conectada com sucesso")
            
            return self.embeddings
            
        except Exception as e:
            raise EmbeddingError(f"Falha ao inicializar embeddings: {e}")
    
    def _sanitize_metadata(self, documents: List[Document]) -> List[Document]:
        """Sanitiza metadados para compatibilidade com Chroma."""
        cleaned_documents = []
        
        for doc in documents:
            safe_metadata = {}
            for key, value in doc.metadata.items():
                try:
                    json.dumps(value)  # Testa se Ã© serializÃ¡vel
                    safe_metadata[key] = value
                except (TypeError, ValueError):
                    safe_metadata[key] = str(value)
            
            doc.metadata = safe_metadata
            cleaned_documents.append(doc)
        
        return cleaned_documents
    
    def load_existing_vector_store(self) -> Optional[Chroma]:
        """Carrega vector store existente se disponÃ­vel."""
        try:
            if not self.embeddings:
                self.initialize_embeddings()
                
            self.vector_store = Chroma(
                persist_directory=str(settings.chroma_path),
                embedding_function=self.embeddings,
                collection_name=settings.collection_name,
            )
            
            # Verifica se tem documentos
            collection = self.vector_store._collection
            if collection.count() > 0:
                logger.info(f"Vector store carregado com {collection.count()} documentos")
                return self.vector_store
            else:
                logger.info("Vector store vazio encontrado")
                return None
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"NÃ£o foi possÃ­vel carregar vector store existente: {e}")
            return None
    
    def index_documents(self, documents: List[Document], batch_size: int = 100) -> None:
        """Indexa documentos no vector store."""
        if not documents:
            logger.warning("Nenhum documento fornecido para indexaÃ§Ã£o")
            return
        
        logger.info(f"Iniciando indexaÃ§Ã£o de {len(documents)} documentos")
        self.metrics.start_indexing()
        
        # Sanitizar metadados
        documents = self._sanitize_metadata(documents)
        
        # Inicializar embeddings se necessÃ¡rio
        if not self.embeddings:
            self.initialize_embeddings()
        
        try:
            # Processar em lotes
            total_batches = (len(documents) + batch_size - 1) // batch_size
            
            for i, start_idx in enumerate(range(0, len(documents), batch_size)):
                end_idx = min(start_idx + batch_size, len(documents))
                batch = documents[start_idx:end_idx]
                
                logger.info(f"Processando lote {i+1}/{total_batches} ({len(batch)} documentos)")
                batch_start_time = time.time()
                
                if i == 0 and not self.vector_store:
                    # Primeiro lote - criar vector store
                    self.vector_store = Chroma.from_documents(
                        documents=batch,
                        embedding=self.embeddings,
                        persist_directory=str(settings.chroma_path),
                        collection_name=settings.collection_name,
                    )
                else:
                    # Lotes subsequentes - adicionar ao store existente
                    if not self.vector_store:
                        self.vector_store = self.load_existing_vector_store()
                    
                    if self.vector_store:
                        self.vector_store.add_documents(batch)
                    else:
                        raise VectorStoreError("Vector store nÃ£o disponÃ­vel")
                
                batch_time = time.time() - batch_start_time
                self.metrics.record_batch(len(batch), batch_time)
                
                logger.info(f"Lote {i+1} processado em {batch_time:.2f}s")
            
            # Persistir mudanÃ§as
            if hasattr(self.vector_store, 'persist'):
                self.vector_store.persist()
            
            # Log de mÃ©tricas finais
            summary = self.metrics.get_summary()
            logger.info(f"âœ… IndexaÃ§Ã£o concluÃ­da!")
            logger.info(f"ðŸ“Š Documentos processados: {summary['total_documents']}")
            logger.info(f"â±ï¸  Tempo total: {summary['total_time_seconds']:.2f}s")
            logger.info(f"ðŸš€ Velocidade: {summary['documents_per_second']:.1f} docs/s")
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.metrics.errors_count += 1
            logger.error(f"Erro durante indexaÃ§Ã£o: {e}")
            raise EmbeddingError(f"Falha na indexaÃ§Ã£o: {e}")
    
    def get_vector_store(self) -> Chroma:
        """Retorna vector store, carregando se necessÃ¡rio."""
        if not self.vector_store:
            self.vector_store = self.load_existing_vector_store()
            
        if not self.vector_store:
            raise VectorStoreError("Vector store nÃ£o disponÃ­vel. Execute indexaÃ§Ã£o primeiro.")
            
        return self.vector_store

class EmbeddingMetrics:
    """Coleta mÃ©tricas de performance da indexaÃ§Ã£o."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.start_time: Optional[float] = None
        self.documents_processed: int = 0
        self.errors_count: int = 0
    
    def start_indexing(self):
        self.start_time = time.time()
        self.documents_processed = 0
        self.errors_count = 0
    
    def record_batch(self, batch_size: int, processing_time: float):
        self.documents_processed += batch_size
    
    def get_summary(self) -> dict:
        total_time = time.time() - self.start_time if self.start_time else 0
        return {
            "total_documents": self.documents_processed,
            "total_time_seconds": total_time,
            "documents_per_second": self.documents_processed / total_time if total_time > 0 else 0,
            "errors": self.errors_count,
        }

def main():
    """FunÃ§Ã£o principal para teste do embedding manager."""
    logger.info("=== TESTE DO EMBEDDING MANAGER ===")
    
    try:
        # Carregar documentos
        loader = DocumentLoader()
        documents = loader.get_document_chunks()
        
        if not documents:
            logger.error("Nenhum documento encontrado para indexaÃ§Ã£o")
            return
        
        # Indexar documentos
        embedding_manager = EmbeddingManager()
        embedding_manager.index_documents(documents)
        
        # Testar recuperaÃ§Ã£o
        vector_store = embedding_manager.get_vector_store()
        test_results = vector_store.similarity_search("teste", k=3)
        logger.info(f"Teste de busca retornou {len(test_results)} resultados")
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Erro no teste: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

                print(f"âŒ [APP] Erro: {e}")
                st.error(error_msg)
                st.session_state.messages.append({"role": "assistant", "content": error_msg})

# Divider e exibiÃ§Ã£o do histÃ³rico
st.markdown("---")
for message in st.session_state.messages:
    with st.chat_message(message["role"]):
        if message["role"] == "user":
            st.markdown(f"<div class='user-message-25'>{message['content']}</div>", unsafe_allow_html=True)
        else:
            st.markdown(message["content"])

# BotÃ£o para limpar conversa
if st.session_state.messages:
    if st.button("ðŸ—‘ï¸ Limpar conversa"):
        st.session_state.messages = []
        st.rerun()

# SOBRE A AIAMIGA
with st.expander("â„¹ï¸ Sobre a AiAmiga"):
    st.markdown("""
    **AiAmiga** Ã© uma assistente especializada em Crediamigo que utiliza:
    - ðŸ§  **Busca SemÃ¢ntica TF-IDF** - Encontra documentos semanticamente relacionados
    - ï¿½ï¿½ Base de conhecimento Crediamigo
    - ðŸ” Busca inteligente com fallback
    - ðŸ’¬ Interface conversacional

    - ðŸ“Š Logs detalhados para debugging
    """)

    page_title="AiAmiga",
    #page_icon="ðŸ¤–",

# FunÃ§Ã£o para carregar CSS
def load_css():
    css_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "styles.css")
    if os.path.exists(css_path):
        with open(css_path, encoding="utf-8") as f:
            st.markdown(f"<style>{f.read()}</style>", unsafe_allow_html=True)
    else:
        st.warning("Arquivo styles.css nÃ£o encontrado!")

# â† NOVA FUNÃ‡ÃƒO
def load_image_as_base64(image_path):
    """Converte imagem para base64."""
    try:
        with open(image_path, "rb") as img_file:
            return base64.b64encode(img_file.read()).decode()
    except FileNotFoundError:
        st.warning(f"Imagem nÃ£o encontrada: {image_path}")
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        st.error(f"Erro ao carregar imagem: {e}")
        return None

# --- INPUT DO USUÃRIO ---

with st.form("chat_form", clear_on_submit=True):
    col1, col2 = st.columns([4, 1])

    with col1:
        user_input = st.text_input(
            "Digite sua pergunta:",
            placeholder="Ex: O que Ã© o Crediamigo?",
            label_visibility="collapsed",
        )

    with col2:
        submit_button = st.form_submit_button("Enviar ðŸš€", use_container_width=True)

# --- PROCESSAR PERGUNTA ---
if submit_button and user_input:
    # Adicionar pergunta do usuÃ¡rio ao histÃ³rico
    st.session_state.messages.append({"role": "user", "content": user_input})

    # Exibir pergunta do usuÃ¡rio
    st.markdown(
        f'<div class="chat-message user-message"><strong>ðŸ‘¤ VocÃª:</strong><br>{user_input}</div>',
        unsafe_allow_html=True,
    )

    # Mostrar loading
    with st.spinner("ðŸ¤– Processando sua pergunta..."):
        try:
            start_time = time.time()
            response = answer_question(user_input)
            end_time = time.time()

            # Adicionar resposta ao histÃ³rico
            st.session_state.messages.append({"role": "assistant", "content": response})

            # Exibir resposta
            st.markdown(
                f'<div class="chat-message assistant-message"><strong>ðŸ¤– AiAmiga:</strong><br>{response}</div>',
                unsafe_allow_html=True,
            )

            # Mostrar tempo de resposta
            response_time = round(end_time - start_time, 2)
            st.caption(f"â±ï¸ Tempo de resposta: {response_time}s")

        except Exception as e:
            error_msg = f"Desculpe, ocorreu um erro ao processar sua pergunta: {str(e)}"
            st.session_state.messages.append({"role": "assistant", "content": error_msg})
            st.error(error_msg)

# --- BOTÃ•ES DE AÃ‡ÃƒO ---
st.markdown("## ðŸ”§ AÃ§Ãµes")
col1, col2, col3 = st.columns(3)

with col1:
    if st.button("ðŸ§¹ Limpar Conversa", use_container_width=True):
        st.session_state.messages = [
            {"role": "assistant", "content": "Conversa limpa! Como posso ajudÃ¡-lo agora?"}
        ]
        st.rerun()

with col2:
    if st.button("ðŸ“Š EstatÃ­sticas", use_container_width=True):
        total_messages = len(st.session_state.messages)
        user_messages = len([m for m in st.session_state.messages if m["role"] == "user"])
        st.info(f"ðŸ“ˆ Total de mensagens: {total_messages}\nðŸ‘¤ Suas perguntas: {user_messages}")

with col3:
    if st.button("ðŸ’¾ Exportar Chat", use_container_width=True):
        chat_export = "\n".join(
            [
                f"{'ðŸ‘¤ VOCÃŠ' if m['role'] == 'user' else 'ðŸ¤– AiAmiga'}: {m['content']}"
                for m in st.session_state.messages
            ]
        )
        st.download_button(
            label="ðŸ“¥ Download do Chat",
            data=chat_export,
            file_name="chat_AiAmiga.txt",
            mime="text/plain",
        )

# --- FOOTER ---
st.markdown("---")
st.markdown(
    "<div style='text-align: center; color: #666;'>"
    "ðŸ¤– AiAmiga - Assistente RAG para Crediamigo | "
    "Desenvolvido com Streamlit + LangChain + OpenAI"
    "</div>",
    unsafe_allow_html=True,
)
